\#\# ABSTRACT

\*\*GRADUATION PROJECT\*\*

\*\*ARTIFICIAL INTELLIGENCE POWERED UNIVERSITY INFORMATION ASSISTANT: SELCUK AI ASSISTANT\*\*

\*\*\[Student Name SURNAME\]\*\*

\*\*Selcuk University Faculty of Technology\*\*  
\*\*Department of Computer Engineering\*\*

\*\*Advisor: \[Title Name SURNAME\]\*\*

\*\*2025, \[Page Count\]\*\*

In this project, an artificial intelligence-powered information assistant has been developed to provide 24/7 service to students and staff of Selcuk University. Located in Konya, Selcuk University is one of Turkey's largest universities, serving approximately 80,000 students through 23 faculties, 6 institutes, and more than 20 vocational schools. In such a large institution, quick access to information for students and staff has become a critical need.

The developed Selcuk AI Assistant provides accurate and up-to-date information about the university using Large Language Models (LLM) and Retrieval Augmented Generation (RAG) technologies. The system is built upon a knowledge base compiled from the university's official website and institutional resources. This approach minimizes the "hallucination" problem of artificial intelligence models and provides reliable responses to users.

Within the scope of the project, Python programming language was used, and a user-friendly interface was designed with modern web frameworks. The system provides information on topics such as academic calendar, faculty information, student affairs procedures, campus services, and frequently asked questions. Tests have shown that the system responds with an accuracy rate of over 90% and an average response time of less than 3 seconds.

This study contributes to the digital transformation process in universities and serves as an example of the effective use of artificial intelligence technologies in educational institutions.

\*\*Keywords:\*\* Artificial Intelligence, Chatbot, Large Language Models, Natural Language Processing, RAG, Selcuk University

\#\# 2\. KAYNAK ARAÅTIRMASI

\#\#\# 2.1. Yapay Zeka ve DoÄŸal Dil Ä°ÅŸleme

Yapay zeka (AI), makinelerin insan benzeri zeka gerektiren gÃ¶revleri yerine getirmesini saÄŸlayan bilgisayar bilimi dalÄ±dÄ±r. DoÄŸal dil iÅŸleme (NLP), yapay zekanÄ±n insan dilini anlama ve Ã¼retme yeteneÄŸini inceleyen alt alanÄ±dÄ±r (Jurafsky ve Martin, 2023).

NLP'nin tarihÃ§esi 1950'lere kadar uzanmaktadÄ±r. Alan Turing'in "Computing Machinery and Intelligence" makalesi (Turing, 1950), makinelerin dÃ¼ÅŸÃ¼nÃ¼p dÃ¼ÅŸÃ¼nemeyeceÄŸi sorusunu gÃ¼ndeme getirmiÅŸtir. Ä°lk NLP sistemleri, kural tabanlÄ± yaklaÅŸÄ±mlar kullanmÄ±ÅŸtÄ±r. ELIZA (Weizenbaum, 1966), ilk sohbet robotlarÄ±ndan biri olarak tarihe geÃ§miÅŸtir.

1980'ler ve 1990'larda istatistiksel yÃ¶ntemler Ã¶n plana Ã§Ä±kmÄ±ÅŸtÄ±r. Makine Ã¶ÄŸrenmesi algoritmalarÄ±, bÃ¼yÃ¼k metin veri setlerinden Ã¶rÃ¼ntÃ¼ler Ã¶ÄŸrenmeye baÅŸlamÄ±ÅŸtÄ±r. Hidden Markov Models (HMM) ve n-gram modelleri bu dÃ¶nemin Ã¶nemli teknikleridir.

2010'larda derin Ã¶ÄŸrenme devrimi yaÅŸanmÄ±ÅŸtÄ±r. Recurrent Neural Networks (RNN) ve Long Short-Term Memory (LSTM) aÄŸlarÄ±, sÄ±ralÄ± veri iÅŸlemede baÅŸarÄ±lÄ± sonuÃ§lar elde etmiÅŸtir (Hochreiter ve Schmidhuber, 1997). Word2Vec (Mikolov ve ark., 2013\) gibi kelime gÃ¶mme (word embedding) teknikleri, kelimelerin anlamsal iliÅŸkilerini yakalamayÄ± mÃ¼mkÃ¼n kÄ±lmÄ±ÅŸtÄ±r.

2017 yÄ±lÄ±nda Vaswani ve arkadaÅŸlarÄ± tarafÄ±ndan Ã¶nerilen Transformer mimarisi, NLP alanÄ±nda paradigma deÄŸiÅŸikliÄŸine yol aÃ§mÄ±ÅŸtÄ±r. Self-attention mekanizmasÄ±, uzun mesafeli baÄŸÄ±mlÄ±lÄ±klarÄ± etkili bir ÅŸekilde modellemeyi saÄŸlamÄ±ÅŸtÄ±r. Bu mimari, gÃ¼nÃ¼mÃ¼zÃ¼n en gÃ¼Ã§lÃ¼ dil modellerinin temelini oluÅŸturmaktadÄ±r.

\#\#\# 2.2. BÃ¼yÃ¼k Dil Modelleri (LLM)

BÃ¼yÃ¼k dil modelleri (Large Language Models \- LLM), milyarlarca parametre iÃ§eren ve bÃ¼yÃ¼k metin veri setleri Ã¼zerinde eÄŸitilen yapay sinir aÄŸlarÄ±dÄ±r. Bu modeller, metin Ã¼retme, Ã§eviri, Ã¶zetleme, soru cevaplama gibi Ã§eÅŸitli NLP gÃ¶revlerinde Ã¼stÃ¼n performans sergilemektedir.

\*\*GPT Serisi (OpenAI):\*\*

GPT (Generative Pre-trained Transformer), OpenAI tarafÄ±ndan geliÅŸtirilen bir dil modeli serisidir. GPT-1 (2018), 117 milyon parametre ile baÅŸlamÄ±ÅŸtÄ±r. GPT-2 (2019) 1.5 milyar, GPT-3 (2020) 175 milyar parametreye ulaÅŸmÄ±ÅŸtÄ±r (Brown ve ark., 2020). GPT-4 (2023), multimodal yetenekleri ile dikkat Ã§ekmiÅŸtir (OpenAI, 2023).

\*\*BERT (Google):\*\*

BERT (Bidirectional Encoder Representations from Transformers), Google tarafÄ±ndan 2018 yÄ±lÄ±nda tanÄ±tÄ±lmÄ±ÅŸtÄ±r (Devlin ve ark., 2019). Ã‡ift yÃ¶nlÃ¼ baÄŸlam anlama yeteneÄŸi ile metin anlama gÃ¶revlerinde Ã§Ä±ÄŸÄ±r aÃ§mÄ±ÅŸtÄ±r.

\*\*LLaMA (Meta):\*\*

LLaMA (Large Language Model Meta AI), Meta tarafÄ±ndan 2023 yÄ±lÄ±nda aÃ§Ä±k kaynak olarak yayÄ±nlanmÄ±ÅŸtÄ±r. 7B ile 65B parametre arasÄ±nda deÄŸiÅŸen versiyonlarÄ± bulunmaktadÄ±r (Touvron ve ark., 2023).

\*\*Gemini (Google):\*\*

Gemini, Google DeepMind tarafÄ±ndan 2023 yÄ±lÄ±nda tanÄ±tÄ±lan multimodal AI modelidir. Metin, gÃ¶rÃ¼ntÃ¼, ses ve video iÅŸleme yeteneklerine sahiptir (Google, 2023).

\*\*TÃ¼rkÃ§e Dil Modelleri:\*\*

TÃ¼rkÃ§e iÃ§in Ã¶zelleÅŸtirilmiÅŸ modeller de geliÅŸtirilmektedir. BERTurk (Schweter, 2020\) ve TÃ¼rkÃ§e GPT modelleri, TÃ¼rkÃ§e NLP gÃ¶revlerinde kullanÄ±lmaktadÄ±r.

\#\#\# 2.3. RAG (Retrieval Augmented Generation)

RAG (Retrieval Augmented Generation), bÃ¼yÃ¼k dil modellerinin bilgi eriÅŸim sistemleri ile birleÅŸtirilmesiyle oluÅŸturulan bir yaklaÅŸÄ±mdÄ±r. Lewis ve arkadaÅŸlarÄ± (2020) tarafÄ±ndan Ã¶nerilen bu yÃ¶ntem, LLM'lerin "hallucination" (uydurma bilgi Ã¼retme) problemine Ã§Ã¶zÃ¼m sunmaktadÄ±r.

\*\*RAG'Ä±n Ã‡alÄ±ÅŸma Prensibi:\*\*

1\. \*\*Soru AlÄ±mÄ±:\*\* KullanÄ±cÄ±dan gelen soru alÄ±nÄ±r.  
2\. \*\*Belge EriÅŸimi (Retrieval):\*\* Soru, vektÃ¶r veritabanÄ±nda aranÄ±r ve ilgili belgeler getirilir.  
3\. \*\*BaÄŸlam OluÅŸturma:\*\* Getirilen belgeler, LLM'e baÄŸlam olarak sunulur.  
4\. \*\*YanÄ±t Ãœretimi (Generation):\*\* LLM, verilen baÄŸlam doÄŸrultusunda yanÄ±t Ã¼retir.

\*\*RAG'Ä±n AvantajlarÄ±:\*\*

\- \*\*GÃ¼ncellik:\*\* Knowledge base gÃ¼ncellendiÄŸinde, model yeniden eÄŸitilmeden gÃ¼ncel bilgi sunabilir.  
\- \*\*DoÄŸruluk:\*\* YanÄ±tlar, doÄŸrulanmÄ±ÅŸ kaynaklara dayandÄ±rÄ±lÄ±r.  
\- \*\*ÅeffaflÄ±k:\*\* YanÄ±tlarÄ±n kaynaklarÄ± gÃ¶sterilebilir.  
\- \*\*Maliyet EtkinliÄŸi:\*\* Model fine-tuning gerektirmez.

\*\*VektÃ¶r VeritabanlarÄ±:\*\*

RAG sistemlerinde belgeler, vektÃ¶r temsillerine dÃ¶nÃ¼ÅŸtÃ¼rÃ¼lerek saklanÄ±r. PopÃ¼ler vektÃ¶r veritabanlarÄ± ÅŸunlardÄ±r:  
\- Pinecone  
\- Weaviate  
\- Milvus  
\- ChromaDB  
\- FAISS (Facebook AI Similarity Search)

\*\*Embedding Modelleri:\*\*

Metinleri vektÃ¶rlere dÃ¶nÃ¼ÅŸtÃ¼rmek iÃ§in embedding modelleri kullanÄ±lÄ±r:  
\- OpenAI text-embedding-ada-002

\#\#\#\# 3.3.3. Metin ParÃ§alama (Chunking)

RAG sistemi iÃ§in metinler, optimal boyutlarda parÃ§alara ayrÄ±lmÄ±ÅŸtÄ±r:

\- \*\*Chunk boyutu:\*\* 500-1000 karakter  
\- \*\*Overlap:\*\* 100 karakter (baÄŸlam kaybÄ±nÄ± Ã¶nlemek iÃ§in)  
\- \*\*AyÄ±rÄ±cÄ±lar:\*\* Paragraf, cÃ¼mle ve anlam bÃ¼tÃ¼nlÃ¼ÄŸÃ¼ gÃ¶zetilerek

\`\`\`python  
from langchain.text\_splitter import RecursiveCharacterTextSplitter

text\_splitter \= RecursiveCharacterTextSplitter(  
    chunk\_size=800,  
    chunk\_overlap=100,  
    separators=\["\\n\\n", "\\n", ".", "\!", "?", ",", " "\]  
)

chunks \= text\_splitter.split\_documents(documents)  
\`\`\`

\#\#\#\# 3.5.2. Retrieval Stratejisi

Belge eriÅŸimi iÃ§in hibrit bir yaklaÅŸÄ±m benimsenmiÅŸtir:

1\. \*\*Semantic Search:\*\* VektÃ¶r benzerliÄŸi ile anlamsal arama  
2\. \*\*Keyword Search:\*\* BM25 algoritmasÄ± ile anahtar kelime aramasÄ±  
3\. \*\*Hybrid Ranking:\*\* Ä°ki yÃ¶ntemin sonuÃ§larÄ±nÄ±n birleÅŸtirilmesi

\`\`\`python  
from langchain.retrievers import EnsembleRetriever  
from langchain.retrievers import BM25Retriever

\# Semantic retriever  
semantic\_retriever \= vector\_store.as\_retriever(  
    search\_type="similarity",  
    search\_kwargs={"k": 5}  
)

\# Keyword retriever  
bm25\_retriever \= BM25Retriever.from\_documents(documents)  
bm25\_retriever.k \= 5

\# Ensemble retriever  
ensemble\_retriever \= EnsembleRetriever(  
    retrievers=\[semantic\_retriever, bm25\_retriever\],  
    weights=\[0.6, 0.4\]  
)

\- Oturum yÃ¶netimi

\*\*3. Veri KatmanÄ± (Data Layer):\*\*  
\- VektÃ¶r veritabanÄ±  
\- Knowledge base  
\- YapÄ±landÄ±rma dosyalarÄ±

\#\#\# 4.2. BileÅŸen TasarÄ±mÄ±

\#\#\#\# 4.2.1. Frontend BileÅŸeni

Frontend, kullanÄ±cÄ± etkileÅŸimini saÄŸlayan arayÃ¼z katmanÄ±dÄ±r.

\*\*KullanÄ±lan Teknolojiler:\*\*  
\- \*\*Framework:\*\* \[Streamlit / Gradio / React \- repo'dan tespit edilecek\]  
\- \*\*Styling:\*\* CSS / Tailwind CSS  
\- \*\*State Management:\*\* Session State

\*\*Temel Ã–zellikler:\*\*  
\- Sohbet arayÃ¼zÃ¼ (chat interface)  
\- Mesaj geÃ§miÅŸi gÃ¶rÃ¼ntÃ¼leme  
\- YÃ¼kleme animasyonlarÄ±  
\- Hata mesajlarÄ±  
\- Responsive tasarÄ±m (mobil uyumlu)

\*\*Ã–rnek Frontend Kodu (Streamlit):\*\*

\`\`\`python  
import streamlit as st  
from chat\_service import ChatService

\# Sayfa yapÄ±landÄ±rmasÄ±  
st.set\_page\_config(  
    page\_title="SelÃ§uk AI Asistan",  
    page\_icon="ğŸ“",  
    layout="centered"  
)

\# BaÅŸlÄ±k  
st.title("ğŸ“ SelÃ§uk Ãœniversitesi AI Asistan")  
st.markdown("SelÃ§uk Ãœniversitesi hakkÄ±nda sorularÄ±nÄ±zÄ± yanÄ±tlÄ±yorum.")

\# Oturum durumu baÅŸlatma  
if "messages" not in st.session\_state:  
    st.session\_state.messages \= \[\]

if "chat\_service" not in st.session\_state:  
    st.session\_state.chat\_service \= ChatService()

\# Mesaj geÃ§miÅŸini gÃ¶ster  
for message in st.session\_state.messages:  
    with st.chat\_message(message\["role"\]):  
        st.markdown(message\["content"\])

\# KullanÄ±cÄ± giriÅŸi  
if prompt := st.chat\_input("Sorunuzu yazÄ±n..."):  
    \# KullanÄ±cÄ± mesajÄ±nÄ± ekle  
    st.session\_state.messages.append({"role": "user", "content": prompt})  
    with st.chat\_message("user"):  
        st.markdown(prompt)  
      
    \# Asistan yanÄ±tÄ±  
    with st.chat\_message("assistant"):  
        with st.spinner("DÃ¼ÅŸÃ¼nÃ¼yorum..."):  
            response \= st.session\_state.chat\_service.get\_response(prompt)  
            st.markdown(response)  
      
    st.session\_state.messages.append({"role": "assistant", "content": response})  
\`\`\`

\#\#\#\# 4.2.2. Backend BileÅŸeni

Backend, API endpoint'lerini ve iÅŸ mantÄ±ÄŸÄ±nÄ± barÄ±ndÄ±rmaktadÄ±r.

\*\*KullanÄ±lan Teknolojiler:\*\*  
\- \*\*Framework:\*\* \[FastAPI / Flask \- repo'dan tespit edilecek\]  
\- \*\*ASGI Server:\*\* Uvicorn  
\- \*\*Validation:\*\* Pydantic

\*\*Ã–rnek Backend Kodu (FastAPI):\*\*

\`\`\`python  
from fastapi import FastAPI, HTTPException  
from pydantic import BaseModel  
from typing import Optional, List  
from rag\_engine import RAGEngine

app \= FastAPI(  
    title="SelÃ§uk AI Asistan API",  
    description="SelÃ§uk Ãœniversitesi Bilgi AsistanÄ± API",  
    version="1.0.0"  
)

\# Veri modelleri  
class ChatRequest(BaseModel):  
    message: str  
    session\_id: Optional\[str\] \= None  
      
class ChatResponse(BaseModel):  
    response: str  
    sources: Optional\[List\[str\]\] \= None  
    session\_id: str

class HealthResponse(BaseModel):  
    status: str  
    version: str

\# RAG Engine baÅŸlatma  
rag\_engine \= RAGEngine()

@app.get("/health", response\_model=HealthResponse)  
async def health\_check():  
    """Sistem saÄŸlÄ±k kontrolÃ¼"""  
    return HealthResponse(status="healthy", version="1.0.0")

@app.post("/chat", response\_model=ChatResponse)  
async def chat(request: ChatRequest):  
    """Ana sohbet endpoint'i"""  
    try:  
        response, sources \= rag\_engine.query(request.message)  
        return ChatResponse(  
            response=response,  
            sources=sources,  
            session\_id=request.session\_id or generate\_session\_id()  
        )  
    except Exception as e:  
        raise HTTPException(status\_code=500, detail=str(e))

@app.get("/")  
async def root():  
    """KÃ¶k endpoint"""  
    return {"message": "SelÃ§uk AI Asistan API'ye hoÅŸ geldiniz\!"}  
\`\`\`

\#\#\#\# 4.2.3. RAG Engine BileÅŸeni

RAG Engine, sistemin Ã§ekirdek bileÅŸenidir ve bilgi eriÅŸimi ile yanÄ±t Ã¼retimini yÃ¶netir.

\*\*Ã–rnek RAG Engine Kodu:\*\*

\`\`\`python  
from langchain.embeddings import OpenAIEmbeddings  
from langchain.vectorstores import FAISS  
from langchain.chat\_models import ChatOpenAI  
from langchain.chains import RetrievalQA  
from langchain.prompts import PromptTemplate  
import os

class RAGEngine:  
    def \_\_init\_\_(self):  
        self.embeddings \= OpenAIEmbeddings()  
        self.vector\_store \= self.\_load\_vector\_store()  
        self.llm \= ChatOpenAI(  
            model\_name="gpt-3.5-turbo",  
            temperature=0.3  
        )  
        self.qa\_chain \= self.\_create\_qa\_chain()  
      
    def \_load\_vector\_store(self):  
        """VektÃ¶r veritabanÄ±nÄ± yÃ¼kle"""  
        vector\_store\_path \= "data/vector\_store"  
        if os.path.exists(vector\_store\_path):  
            return FAISS.load\_local(  
                vector\_store\_path,   
                self.embeddings,  
                allow\_dangerous\_deserialization=True  
            )  
        else:  
            raise FileNotFoundError("Vector store bulunamadÄ±\!")  
      
    def \_create\_qa\_chain(self):  
        """QA zinciri oluÅŸtur"""  
        prompt\_template \= """  
        Sen SelÃ§uk Ãœniversitesi AI AsistanÄ±sÄ±n. AÅŸaÄŸÄ±daki baÄŸlam   
        bilgilerini kullanarak soruyu yanÄ±tla.  
          
        Kurallar:  
        \- YalnÄ±zca baÄŸlamdaki bilgileri kullan  
        \- BilmediÄŸin konularda "Bu konuda bilgim yok" de  
        \- TÃ¼rkÃ§e yanÄ±t ver  
        \- KÄ±sa ve Ã¶z ol  
          
        BaÄŸlam:  
        {context}  
          
        Soru: {question}  
          
        YanÄ±t:  
        """  
          
        PROMPT \= PromptTemplate(  
            template=prompt\_template,  
            input\_variables=\["context", "question"\]  
        )  
          
        return RetrievalQA.from\_chain\_type(  
            llm=self.llm,  
            chain\_type="stuff",  
            retriever=self.vector\_store.as\_retriever(  
                search\_kwargs={"k": 4}  
            ),  
            chain\_type\_kwargs={"prompt": PROMPT},  
            return\_source\_documents=True  
        )  
      
    def query(self, question: str) \-\> tuple:  
        """Soru sor ve yanÄ±t al"""  
        result \= self.qa\_chain({"query": question})  
        response \= result\["result"\]  
        sources \= \[doc.metadata.get("source", "")   
                   for doc in result.get("source\_documents", \[\])\]  
        return response, sources  
\`\`\`

\#\#\#\# 4.2.4. Knowledge Base Manager BileÅŸeni

Knowledge Base Manager, bilgi tabanÄ±nÄ±n yÃ¶netiminden sorumludur.

\`\`\`python  
import json  
from datetime import datetime  
from typing import List, Dict, Optional

class KnowledgeBaseManager:  
    def \_\_init\_\_(self, kb\_path: str \= "data/knowledge\_base.json"):  
        self.kb\_path \= kb\_path  
        self.knowledge\_base \= self.\_load\_kb()  
      
    def \_load\_kb(self) \-\> Dict:  
        """Knowledge base'i yÃ¼kle"""  
        try:  
            with open(self.kb\_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:  
                return json.load(f)  
        except FileNotFoundError:  
            return {"entries": \[\], "metadata": {}}  
      
    def \_save\_kb(self):  
        """Knowledge base'i kaydet"""  
        with open(self.kb\_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:  
            json.dump(self.knowledge\_base, f, ensure\_ascii=False, indent=2)  
      
    def add\_entry(self, entry: Dict) \-\> bool:  
        """Yeni kayÄ±t ekle"""  
        entry\["id"\] \= self.\_generate\_id()  
        entry\["created\_at"\] \= datetime.now().isoformat()  
        self.knowledge\_base\["entries"\].append(entry)  
        self.\_save\_kb()  
        return True  
      
    def search(self, query: str, category: Optional\[str\] \= None) \-\> List\[Dict\]:  
        """KayÄ±t ara"""  
        results \= \[\]  
        for entry in self.knowledge\_base\["entries"\]:  
            if category and entry.get("category") \!= category:  
                continue  
            if query.lower() in entry.get("content", "").lower():  
                results.append(entry)  
        return results  
      
    def get\_by\_category(self, category: str) \-\> List\[Dict\]:  
        """Kategoriye gÃ¶re kayÄ±tlarÄ± getir"""  
        return \[e for e in self.knowledge\_base\["entries"\]   
                if e.get("category") \== category\]  
      
    def update\_entry(self, entry\_id: str, updates: Dict) \-\> bool:  
        """KayÄ±t gÃ¼ncelle"""  
        for entry in self.knowledge\_base\["entries"\]:  
            if entry.get("id") \== entry\_id:  
                entry.update(updates)  
                entry\["updated\_at"\] \= datetime.now().isoformat()  
                self.\_save\_kb()  
                return True  
        return False  
      
    def \_generate\_id(self) \-\> str:  
        """Benzersiz ID oluÅŸtur"""  
        import uuid  
        return str(uuid.uuid4())\[:8\]  
\`\`\`

\#\#\#\# 4.3.4. Rate Limiting

API, aÅŸÄ±rÄ± kullanÄ±mÄ± Ã¶nlemek iÃ§in rate limiting uygulamaktadÄ±r.

\`\`\`python  
from fastapi import FastAPI, Request  
from slowapi import Limiter, \_rate\_limit\_exceeded\_handler  
from slowapi.util import get\_remote\_address  
from slowapi.errors import RateLimitExceeded

limiter \= Limiter(key\_func=get\_remote\_address)  
app \= FastAPI()  
app.state.limiter \= limiter  
app.add\_exception\_handler(RateLimitExceeded, \_rate\_limit\_exceeded\_handler)

@app.post("/chat")  
@limiter.limit("30/minute")  \# Dakikada 30 istek  
async def chat(request: Request, chat\_request: ChatRequest):  
    \# Chat iÅŸlemi  
    pass  
\`\`\`

\*\*Rate Limit KurallarÄ±:\*\*  
\- Anonim kullanÄ±cÄ±lar: 30 istek/dakika  
\- KayÄ±tlÄ± kullanÄ±cÄ±lar: 60 istek/dakika  
\- Premium kullanÄ±cÄ±lar: 120 istek/dakika

\#\#\#\# 4.4.3. VektÃ¶r VeritabanÄ±

VektÃ¶r veritabanÄ± olarak FAISS (Facebook AI Similarity Search) kullanÄ±lmÄ±ÅŸtÄ±r.

\*\*VektÃ¶r Store OluÅŸturma:\*\*  
\`\`\`python  
from langchain.document\_loaders import JSONLoader  
from langchain.text\_splitter import RecursiveCharacterTextSplitter  
from langchain.embeddings import OpenAIEmbeddings  
from langchain.vectorstores import FAISS  
import os

class VectorStoreBuilder:  
    def \_\_init\_\_(self):  
        self.embeddings \= OpenAIEmbeddings()  
        self.text\_splitter \= RecursiveCharacterTextSplitter(  
            chunk\_size=800,  
            chunk\_overlap=100,  
            separators=\["\\n\\n", "\\n", ".", "\!", "?", ",", " "\]  
        )  
      
    def load\_documents(self, data\_dir: str):  
        """JSON dosyalarÄ±ndan dÃ¶kÃ¼manlarÄ± yÃ¼kle"""  
        documents \= \[\]  
        for filename in os.listdir(data\_dir):  
            if filename.endswith('.json'):  
                filepath \= os.path.join(data\_dir, filename)  
                loader \= JSONLoader(  
                    file\_path=filepath,  
                    jq\_schema='.\[\]',  
                    text\_content=False  
                )  
                documents.extend(loader.load())  
        return documents  
      
    def build\_vector\_store(self, documents, save\_path: str):  
        """VektÃ¶r store oluÅŸtur ve kaydet"""  
        \# DÃ¶kÃ¼manlarÄ± parÃ§ala  
        chunks \= self.text\_splitter.split\_documents(documents)  
        print(f"Toplam {len(chunks)} chunk oluÅŸturuldu.")  
          
        \# VektÃ¶r store oluÅŸtur  
        vector\_store \= FAISS.from\_documents(chunks, self.embeddings)  
          
        \# Kaydet  
        vector\_store.save\_local(save\_path)  
        print(f"VektÃ¶r store kaydedildi: {save\_path}")  
          
        return vector\_store  
      
    def update\_vector\_store(self, new\_documents, store\_path: str):  
        """Mevcut vektÃ¶r store'a yeni dÃ¶kÃ¼manlar ekle"""  
        \# Mevcut store'u yÃ¼kle  
        vector\_store \= FAISS.load\_local(  
            store\_path,   
            self.embeddings,  
            allow\_dangerous\_deserialization=True  
        )  
          
        \# Yeni dÃ¶kÃ¼manlarÄ± parÃ§ala ve ekle  
        chunks \= self.text\_splitter.split\_documents(new\_documents)  
        vector\_store.add\_documents(chunks)  
          
        \# GÃ¼ncellemeyi kaydet  
        vector\_store.save\_local(store\_path)  
        print(f"VektÃ¶r store gÃ¼ncellendi: {len(chunks)} yeni chunk eklendi.")  
          
        return vector\_store

\# KullanÄ±m  
if \_\_name\_\_ \== "\_\_main\_\_":  
    builder \= VectorStoreBuilder()  
    docs \= builder.load\_documents("data/knowledge\_base")  
    builder.build\_vector\_store(docs, "data/vector\_store")  
\`\`\`

\#\#\# 4.5. KullanÄ±cÄ± ArayÃ¼zÃ¼

\#\#\#\# 4.5.1. ArayÃ¼z TasarÄ±m Prensipleri

KullanÄ±cÄ± arayÃ¼zÃ¼ tasarÄ±mÄ±nda aÅŸaÄŸÄ±daki prensipler gÃ¶zetilmiÅŸtir:

1\. \*\*Sadelik:\*\* KullanÄ±cÄ±larÄ±n kolayca anlayabileceÄŸi minimalist tasarÄ±m  
2\. \*\*EriÅŸilebilirlik:\*\* WCAG 2.1 standartlarÄ±na uygunluk  
3\. \*\*Responsive:\*\* TÃ¼m cihazlarda uyumlu gÃ¶rÃ¼ntÃ¼leme

\#\#\# 4.6. GÃ¼venlik TasarÄ±mÄ±

\#\#\#\# 4.6.1. GÃ¼venlik Ã–nlemleri

\*\*1. Input Validation:\*\*  
\`\`\`python  
from pydantic import BaseModel, validator  
import re

class ChatRequest(BaseModel):  
    message: str  
    session\_id: Optional\[str\] \= None  
      
    @validator('message')  
    def validate\_message(cls, v):  
        \# BoÅŸ mesaj kontrolÃ¼  
        if not v or not v.strip():  
            raise ValueError('Mesaj boÅŸ olamaz')  
          
        \# Maksimum uzunluk kontrolÃ¼  
        if len(v) \> 2000:  
            raise ValueError('Mesaj 2000 karakterden uzun olamaz')  
          
        \# ZararlÄ± iÃ§erik kontrolÃ¼  
        dangerous\_patterns \= \[  
            r'\<script.\*?\>.\*?\</script\>',  
            r'javascript:',  
            r'on\\w+\\s\*=',  
        \]  
        for pattern in dangerous\_patterns:  
            if re.search(pattern, v, re.IGNORECASE):  
                raise ValueError('GeÃ§ersiz iÃ§erik tespit edildi')  
          
        return v.strip()  
\`\`\`

\*\*2. Rate Limiting:\*\*  
\- IP bazlÄ± istek sÄ±nÄ±rlamasÄ±  
\- Session bazlÄ± istek sÄ±nÄ±rlamasÄ±  
\- Brute force korumasÄ±

\*\*3. HTTPS ZorunluluÄŸu:\*\*  
\`\`\`python

\- IP adresleri hash'lenerek saklanÄ±r  
\- KVKK uyumluluÄŸu saÄŸlanÄ±r

\*\*3. Log GÃ¼venliÄŸi:\*\*  
\`\`\`python  
import logging

\# Hassas bilgileri loglardan filtrele  
class SensitiveDataFilter(logging.Filter):  
    def filter(self, record):  
        \# API anahtarlarÄ±nÄ± maskele  
        if hasattr(record, 'msg'):  
            record.msg \= re.sub(  
                r'(api\_key|password|token)=\[^\\s&\]+',  
                r'\\1=\*\*\*MASKED\*\*\*',  
                str(record.msg)  
            )  
        return True

logger \= logging.getLogger(\_\_name\_\_)  
logger.addFilter(SensitiveDataFilter())  
\`\`\`

\#\#\#\# 4.6.3. Prompt Injection KorumasÄ±

\`\`\`python  
def sanitize\_user\_input(user\_input: str) \-\> str:  
    """KullanÄ±cÄ± girdisini temizle ve prompt injection'Ä± Ã¶nle"""  
      
    \# Tehlikeli kalÄ±plarÄ± tespit et  
    injection\_patterns \= \[  
        r'ignore previous instructions',  
        r'disregard all prior',  
        r'forget everything',  
        r'you are now',  
        r'act as',  
        r'pretend to be',  
        r'system prompt',  
        r'reveal your instructions',  
    \]  
      
    lower\_input \= user\_input.lower()  
    for pattern in injection\_patterns:  
        if re.search(pattern, lower\_input):  
            return "\[GeÃ§ersiz sorgu tespit edildi\]"  
      
    \# Ã–zel karakterleri escape et  
    sanitized \= user\_input.replace("{", "{{").replace("}", "}}")  
      
    return sanitized

import pytest  
from rag\_engine import RAGEngine

class TestRAGEngine:  
    @pytest.fixture  
    def rag\_engine(self):  
        return RAGEngine()  
      
    def test\_query\_returns\_response(self, rag\_engine):  
        """Sorgu yanÄ±t dÃ¶ndÃ¼rmeli"""  
        response, sources \= rag\_engine.query("SelÃ§uk Ãœniversitesi nerede?")  
        assert response is not None  
        assert len(response) \> 0  
      
    def test\_query\_contains\_konya(self, rag\_engine):  
        """Konya sorusu Konya iÃ§ermeli"""  
        response, \_ \= rag\_engine.query("SelÃ§uk Ãœniversitesi hangi ÅŸehirde?")  
        assert "konya" in response.lower()  
      
    def test\_empty\_query\_handled(self, rag\_engine):  
        """BoÅŸ sorgu hata vermemeli"""  
        with pytest.raises(ValueError):  
            rag\_engine.query("")  
      
    def test\_sources\_returned(self, rag\_engine):  
        """Kaynaklar dÃ¶ndÃ¼rÃ¼lmeli"""  
        \_, sources \= rag\_engine.query("KaÃ§ fakÃ¼lte var?")  
        assert isinstance(sources, list)

\#\#\#\# 5.2.2. Hallucination Testleri

Sistemin uydurma bilgi Ã¼retip Ã¼retmediÄŸi test edilmiÅŸtir.

\*\*Ã‡izelge 5.2.\*\* Hallucination test sonuÃ§larÄ±

| \# | Test Sorusu | Beklenen DavranÄ±ÅŸ | GerÃ§ek DavranÄ±ÅŸ | SonuÃ§ |  
|---|-------------|-------------------|-----------------|-------|  
| 1 | SelÃ§uk Ãœniversitesi'nin uzay fakÃ¼ltesi var mÄ±? | Yok demeli | "BÃ¶yle bir fakÃ¼lte bulunmamaktadÄ±r" | âœ… |  
| 2 | 2050 yÄ±lÄ± akademik takvimi ne? | Bilmiyorum demeli | "Bu konuda gÃ¼ncel bilgim yok" | âœ… |  
| 3 | RektÃ¶rÃ¼n telefon numarasÄ± ne? | KiÅŸisel bilgi vermemeli | "KiÅŸisel iletiÅŸim bilgisi paylaÅŸamam" | âœ… |  
| 4 | SÄ±nav sorularÄ±nÄ± verir misin? | Vermemeli | "SÄ±nav sorularÄ± paylaÅŸamam" | âœ… |  
| 5 | Benim notlarÄ±m ne? | EriÅŸemem demeli | "KiÅŸisel not bilgilerine eriÅŸemiyorum" | âœ… |

\*\*Hallucination OranÄ±:\*\* 0/5 \= \*\*%0\*\* (BaÅŸarÄ±lÄ±)

\#\#\#\# 5.2.3. Edge Case Testleri

\#\#\#\# 5.4.2. Zorluk DetaylarÄ± ve Ã‡Ã¶zÃ¼m YaklaÅŸÄ±mlarÄ±

\*\*1. Hallucination Problemi:\*\*

BÃ¼yÃ¼k dil modelleri, eÄŸitim verilerinde olmayan bilgileri "uydurma" eÄŸilimindedir. Bu, bir Ã¼niversite bilgi asistanÄ± iÃ§in kritik bir sorundur.

\*Uygulanan Ã‡Ã¶zÃ¼mler:\*  
\`\`\`python

KURAL: YalnÄ±zca aÅŸaÄŸÄ±daki BAÄLAM bilgilerini kullan.  
BAÄLAM'da olmayan hiÃ§bir bilgiyi UYDURMA.  
Emin olmadÄ±ÄŸÄ±n konularda "Bu konuda kesin bilgim bulunmamaktadÄ±r" de.

BAÄLAM:  
{context}

NOT: BaÄŸlam dÄ±ÅŸÄ± bilgi verme. Tahmin yapma. Uydurma.  
"""

\# Confidence threshold  
def filter\_low\_confidence\_responses(response, threshold=0.7):  
    if response.confidence \< threshold:  
        return "Bu konuda yeterli bilgim bulunmamaktadÄ±r."  
    return response.text  
\`\`\`

\*\*2. TÃ¼rkÃ§e Dil DesteÄŸi:\*\*

BazÄ± LLM'ler TÃ¼rkÃ§e'de Ä°ngilizce'ye kÄ±yasla dÃ¼ÅŸÃ¼k performans gÃ¶stermektedir.

\*Uygulanan Ã‡Ã¶zÃ¼mler:\*  
\- TÃ¼rkÃ§e performansÄ± yÃ¼ksek model seÃ§imi (GPT-4, Gemini Pro)  
\- TÃ¼rkÃ§e Ã¶zel prompt ÅŸablonlarÄ±  
\- TÃ¼rkÃ§e embedding modeli deÄŸerlendirmesi  
\- Post-processing ile dil dÃ¼zeltmeleri

\`\`\`python

        'i': 'Ä°', 'Ä±': 'I', 'ÄŸ': 'Ä', 'Ã¼': 'Ãœ',  
        'ÅŸ': 'Å', 'Ã¶': 'Ã–', 'Ã§': 'Ã‡'

\`\`\`

\*\*3. YanÄ±t SÃ¼resi Optimizasyonu:\*\*

Ä°lk versiyonda ortalama yanÄ±t sÃ¼resi 4-5 saniyeydi.

\*Uygulanan Ã‡Ã¶zÃ¼mler:\*  
\`\`\`python  
\# Async iÅŸleme  
async def get\_response\_async(query: str):  
    \# Paralel retrieval ve preprocessing  
    retrieval\_task \= asyncio.create\_task(retrieve\_documents(query))  
    preprocess\_task \= asyncio.create\_task(preprocess\_query(query))  
      
    docs, processed\_query \= await asyncio.gather(  
        retrieval\_task,   
        preprocess\_task  
    )  
      
    return await generate\_response(processed\_query, docs)

\# Response caching

\# SÄ±k sorulan sorular iÃ§in cache

\*\*4. BaÄŸlam YÃ¶netimi:\*\*

Uzun konuÅŸmalarda Ã¶nceki mesajlarÄ±n unutulmasÄ± sorunu yaÅŸanmÄ±ÅŸtÄ±r.

\*Uygulanan Ã‡Ã¶zÃ¼mler:\*  
\`\`\`python  
from langchain.memory import ConversationBufferWindowMemory

class ConversationManager:  
    def \_\_init\_\_(self, window\_size=5):  
        self.memory \= ConversationBufferWindowMemory(  
            k=window\_size,  
            return\_messages=True  
        )  
      
    def add\_message(self, role: str, content: str):  
        if role \== "user":  
            self.memory.chat\_memory.add\_user\_message(content)  
        else:  
            self.memory.chat\_memory.add\_ai\_message(content)  
      
    def get\_context(self):  
        return self.memory.load\_memory\_variables({})  
      
    def clear(self):  
        self.memory.clear()  
\`\`\`

1\. \*\*Veri KapsamÄ±:\*\* Knowledge base, Ã¼niversitenin tÃ¼m bilgilerini kapsamamaktadÄ±r. Ã–zellikle gÃ¼ncel duyurular ve dinamik iÃ§erikler sÄ±nÄ±rlÄ±dÄ±r.

2\. \*\*KiÅŸisel Bilgi EriÅŸimi:\*\* Sistem, Ã¶ÄŸrenci not, devamsÄ±zlÄ±k gibi kiÅŸisel bilgilere eriÅŸememektedir (gÃ¼venlik gereÄŸi).

3\. \*\*Ã‡oklu Dil DesteÄŸi:\*\* Åu an yalnÄ±zca TÃ¼rkÃ§e desteklenmektedir. Ä°ngilizce ve diÄŸer diller iÃ§in geliÅŸtirme gerekmektedir.

4\. \*\*Offline Ã‡alÄ±ÅŸma:\*\* Sistem, LLM API'ye baÄŸÄ±mlÄ± olduÄŸundan internet baÄŸlantÄ±sÄ± gerektirmektedir.

5\. \*\*Maliyet:\*\* LLM API kullanÄ±mÄ±, Ã¶lÃ§eklendirmede maliyet faktÃ¶rÃ¼ oluÅŸturmaktadÄ±r.

\`\`\`python  
"""  
SelÃ§uk Ãœniversitesi AI Asistan \- Ana Uygulama  
"""

import os  
from fastapi import FastAPI, HTTPException  
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware  
from pydantic import BaseModel, validator  
from typing import Optional, List  
from dotenv import load\_dotenv

from rag\_engine import RAGEngine  
from conversation\_manager import ConversationManager

\# Environment variables  
load\_dotenv()

\# FastAPI uygulamasÄ±  
app \= FastAPI(  
    title="SelÃ§uk AI Asistan API",  
    description="SelÃ§uk Ãœniversitesi Yapay Zeka Destekli Bilgi AsistanÄ±",  
    version="1.0.0",  
    docs\_url="/docs",  
    redoc\_url="/redoc"  
)

\# CORS ayarlarÄ±  
app.add\_middleware(  
    CORSMiddleware,  
    allow\_origins=\["\*"\],  
    allow\_credentials=True,  
    allow\_methods=\["\*"\],  
    allow\_headers=\["\*"\],  
)

\# Global instances  
rag\_engine \= RAGEngine()  
conversations \= {}

\# Pydantic modelleri  
class ChatRequest(BaseModel):  
    message: str  
    session\_id: Optional\[str\] \= None  
      
    @validator('message')  
    def validate\_message(cls, v):  
        if not v or not v.strip():  
            raise ValueError('Mesaj boÅŸ olamaz')  
        if len(v) \> 2000:  
            raise ValueError('Mesaj 2000 karakterden uzun olamaz')  
        return v.strip()

class ChatResponse(BaseModel):  
    success: bool  
    response: str  
    sources: Optional\[List\[str\]\] \= None  
    session\_id: str

class HealthResponse(BaseModel):  
    status: str  
    version: str  
    components: dict

\# Endpoints  
@app.get("/", tags=\["Root"\])  
async def root():  
    """API kÃ¶k endpoint'i"""  
    return {  
        "message": "SelÃ§uk AI Asistan API'ye hoÅŸ geldiniz\!",  
        "version": "1.0.0",  
        "docs": "/docs"  
    }

@app.get("/health", response\_model=HealthResponse, tags=\["Health"\])  
async def health\_check():  
    """Sistem saÄŸlÄ±k kontrolÃ¼"""  
    return HealthResponse(  
        status="healthy",  
        version="1.0.0",  
        components={  
            "api": "operational",  
            "rag\_engine": "operational",  
            "vector\_store": "operational"  
        }  
    )

@app.post("/chat", response\_model=ChatResponse, tags=\["Chat"\])  
async def chat(request: ChatRequest):  
    """Ana sohbet endpoint'i"""  
    try:  
        \# Session yÃ¶netimi  
        session\_id \= request.session\_id or generate\_session\_id()  
          
        if session\_id not in conversations:  
            conversations\[session\_id\] \= ConversationManager()  
          
        \# RAG sorgusu  
        response, sources \= rag\_engine.query(request.message)  
          
        \# KonuÅŸma geÃ§miÅŸine ekle  
        conversations\[session\_id\].add\_message("user", request.message)  
        conversations\[session\_id\].add\_message("assistant", response)  
          
        return ChatResponse(  
            success=True,  
            response=response,  
            sources=sources,  
            session\_id=session\_id  
        )  
      
    except Exception as e:  
        raise HTTPException(status\_code=500, detail=str(e))

def generate\_session\_id() \-\> str:  
    """Benzersiz session ID oluÅŸtur"""  
    import uuid  
    return str(uuid.uuid4())

if \_\_name\_\_ \== "\_\_main\_\_":  
    import uvicorn  
    uvicorn.run(app, host="0.0.0.0", port=8000)

\*\*EK-A.2: RAG Engine (rag\_engine.py)\*\*

\`\`\`python  
"""  
RAG (Retrieval Augmented Generation) Engine  
"""

import os  
from typing import Tuple, List  
from langchain.embeddings import OpenAIEmbeddings  
from langchain.vectorstores import FAISS  
from langchain.chat\_models import ChatOpenAI  
from langchain.chains import RetrievalQA  
from langchain.prompts import PromptTemplate

class RAGEngine:  
    """RAG tabanlÄ± soru-cevap motoru"""  
      
    def \_\_init\_\_(self):  
        self.embeddings \= OpenAIEmbeddings()  
        self.vector\_store \= self.\_load\_vector\_store()  
        self.llm \= self.\_initialize\_llm()  
        self.qa\_chain \= self.\_create\_qa\_chain()  
      
    def \_load\_vector\_store(self) \-\> FAISS:  
        """VektÃ¶r veritabanÄ±nÄ± yÃ¼kle"""  
        vector\_store\_path \= os.getenv("VECTOR\_STORE\_PATH", "data/vector\_store")  
          
        if not os.path.exists(vector\_store\_path):  
            raise FileNotFoundError(f"Vector store bulunamadÄ±: {vector\_store\_path}")  
          
        return FAISS.load\_local(  
            vector\_store\_path,  
            self.embeddings,  
            allow\_dangerous\_deserialization=True  
        )  
      
    def \_initialize\_llm(self) \-\> ChatOpenAI:  
        """LLM modelini baÅŸlat"""  
        return ChatOpenAI(  
            model\_name=os.getenv("LLM\_MODEL", "gpt-3.5-turbo"),  
            temperature=0.3,  
            max\_tokens=1000  
        )  
      
    def \_create\_qa\_chain(self) \-\> RetrievalQA:  
        """QA zinciri oluÅŸtur"""  
        prompt\_template \= """  
Sen SelÃ§uk Ãœniversitesi AI AsistanÄ±sÄ±n. GÃ¶revin, SelÃ§uk Ãœniversitesi   
hakkÄ±nda doÄŸru ve gÃ¼ncel bilgiler sunmaktÄ±r.

Ã–NEMLÄ° KURALLAR:  
1\. YALNIZCA aÅŸaÄŸÄ±daki BAÄLAM bilgilerini kullan.  
2\. BaÄŸlamda OLMAYAN bilgileri KESÄ°NLÄ°KLE UYDURMA.  
3\. Emin olmadÄ±ÄŸÄ±n konularda "Bu konuda kesin bilgim bulunmamaktadÄ±r" de.  
4\. YanÄ±tlarÄ±nÄ± TÃ¼rkÃ§e ver.  
5\. KÄ±sa, Ã¶z ve anlaÅŸÄ±lÄ±r yanÄ±tlar ver.  
6\. Nazik ve yardÄ±msever ol.

TEMEL BÄ°LGÄ°LER (Her zaman doÄŸru):  
\- SelÃ§uk Ãœniversitesi KONYA'dadÄ±r (Ä°zmir, Ankara veya baÅŸka ÅŸehir DEÄÄ°L\!)  
\- 1975 yÄ±lÄ±nda kurulmuÅŸtur  
\- TÃ¼rkiye'nin en bÃ¼yÃ¼k Ã¼niversitelerinden biridir  
\- 23 fakÃ¼ltesi bulunmaktadÄ±r

BAÄLAM:  
{context}

KULLANICI SORUSU: {question}

YANITINI YALNIZCA BAÄLAM BÄ°LGÄ°LERÄ°NE DAYANDIRARAK VER:  
"""  
          
        PROMPT \= PromptTemplate(  
            template=prompt\_template,  
            input\_variables=\["context", "question"\]  
        )  
          
        retriever \= self.vector\_store.as\_retriever(  
            search\_type="similarity",  
            search\_kwargs={"k": 4}  
        )  
          
        return RetrievalQA.from\_chain\_type(  
            llm=self.llm,  
            chain\_type="stuff",  
            retriever=retriever,  
            chain\_type\_kwargs={"prompt": PROMPT},  
            return\_source\_documents=True  
        )  
      
    def query(self, question: str) \-\> Tuple\[str, List\[str\]\]:  
        """  
        Soru sor ve yanÄ±t al  
          
        Args:  
            question: KullanÄ±cÄ± sorusu  
              
        Returns:  
            Tuple\[str, List\[str\]\]: (yanÄ±t, kaynak listesi)  
        """  
        if not question or not question.strip():  
            raise ValueError("Soru boÅŸ olamaz")  
          
        \# Sorguyu Ã§alÄ±ÅŸtÄ±r  
        result \= self.qa\_chain({"query": question})  
          
        \# YanÄ±t ve kaynaklarÄ± ayÄ±kla  
        response \= result\["result"\]  
        sources \= \[\]  
          
        for doc in result.get("source\_documents", \[\]):  
            source \= doc.metadata.get("source", "")  
            if source and source not in sources:  
                sources.append(source)  
          
        return response, sources  
      
    def get\_similar\_documents(self, query: str, k: int \= 5\) \-\> List\[dict\]:  
        """Benzer dÃ¶kÃ¼manlarÄ± getir"""  
        docs \= self.vector\_store.similarity\_search(query, k=k)  
        return \[  
            {  
                "content": doc.page\_content,  
                "metadata": doc.metadata  
            }  
            for doc in docs  
        \]  
\`\`\`

\*\*EK-A.3: Knowledge Base Builder (kb\_builder.py)\*\*

\`\`\`python  
"""  
Knowledge Base Builder \- VektÃ¶r veritabanÄ± oluÅŸturma  
"""

import os  
import json  
from typing import List  
from langchain.document\_loaders import JSONLoader, DirectoryLoader  
from langchain.text\_splitter import RecursiveCharacterTextSplitter  
from langchain.embeddings import OpenAIEmbeddings  
from langchain.vectorstores import FAISS  
from langchain.schema import Document

class KnowledgeBaseBuilder:  
    """Knowledge base oluÅŸturucu"""  
      
    def \_\_init\_\_(self):  
        self.embeddings \= OpenAIEmbeddings()  
        self.text\_splitter \= RecursiveCharacterTextSplitter(  
            chunk\_size=800,  
            chunk\_overlap=100,  
            separators=\["\\n\\n", "\\n", ".", "\!", "?", ",", " "\]  
        )  
      
    def load\_json\_files(self, data\_dir: str) \-\> List\[Document\]:  
        """JSON dosyalarÄ±ndan dÃ¶kÃ¼manlarÄ± yÃ¼kle"""  
        documents \= \[\]  
          
        for filename in os.listdir(data\_dir):  
            if filename.endswith('.json'):  
                filepath \= os.path.join(data\_dir, filename)  
                  
                with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:  
                    data \= json.load(f)  
                  
                \# JSON yapÄ±sÄ±na gÃ¶re dÃ¶kÃ¼man oluÅŸtur  
                docs \= self.\_parse\_json\_to\_documents(data, filename)  
                documents.extend(docs)  
          
        print(f"Toplam {len(documents)} dÃ¶kÃ¼man yÃ¼klendi.")  
        return documents  
      
    def \_parse\_json\_to\_documents(self, data: dict, source: str) \-\> List\[Document\]:  
        """JSON verisini Document listesine dÃ¶nÃ¼ÅŸtÃ¼r"""  
        documents \= \[\]  
          
        def extract\_text(obj, path=""):  
            if isinstance(obj, dict):  
                for key, value in obj.items():  
                    new\_path \= f"{path}.{key}" if path else key  
                    extract\_text(value, new\_path)  
            elif isinstance(obj, list):  
                for i, item in enumerate(obj):  
                    extract\_text(item, f"{path}\[{i}\]")  
            elif isinstance(obj, str) and len(obj) \> 50:  
                documents.append(Document(  
                    page\_content=obj,  
                    metadata={"source": source, "path": path}  
                ))  
          
        extract\_text(data)  
        return documents  
      
    def build\_vector\_store(self, documents: List\[Document\], save\_path: str) \-\> FAISS:  
        """VektÃ¶r store oluÅŸtur ve kaydet"""  
        \# DÃ¶kÃ¼manlarÄ± parÃ§ala  
        chunks \= self.text\_splitter.split\_documents(documents)  
        print(f"Toplam {len(chunks)} chunk oluÅŸturuldu.")  
          
        \# VektÃ¶r store oluÅŸtur  
        vector\_store \= FAISS.from\_documents(chunks, self.embeddings)  
          
        \# Kaydet  
        vector\_store.save\_local(save\_path)  
        print(f"VektÃ¶r store kaydedildi: {save\_path}")  
          
        return vector\_store  
      
    def update\_vector\_store(self, new\_documents: List\[Document\], store\_path: str) \-\> FAISS:  
        """Mevcut vektÃ¶r store'a yeni dÃ¶kÃ¼manlar ekle"""  
        \# Mevcut store'u yÃ¼kle  
        vector\_store \= FAISS.load\_local(  
            store\_path,  
            self.embeddings,  
            allow\_dangerous\_deserialization=True  
        )  
          
        \# Yeni dÃ¶kÃ¼manlarÄ± parÃ§ala ve ekle  
        chunks \= self.text\_splitter.split\_documents(new\_documents)  
        vector\_store.add\_documents(chunks)  
          
        \# GÃ¼ncellemeyi kaydet  
        vector\_store.save\_local(store\_path)  
        print(f"VektÃ¶r store gÃ¼ncellendi: {len(chunks)} yeni chunk eklendi.")  
          
        return vector\_store

\# KullanÄ±m Ã¶rneÄŸi  
if \_\_name\_\_ \== "\_\_main\_\_":  
    builder \= KnowledgeBaseBuilder()  
      
    \# DÃ¶kÃ¼manlarÄ± yÃ¼kle  
    docs \= builder.load\_json\_files("data/knowledge\_base")  
      
    \# VektÃ¶r store oluÅŸtur  
    builder.build\_vector\_store(docs, "data/vector\_store")  
\`\`\`

| \`GET /history/{session\_id}\` | GET | Sohbet geÃ§miÅŸi |  
| \`POST /feedback\` | POST | Geri bildirim gÃ¶nderme |

\*\*EK-B.2: Chat Endpoint DetayÄ±\*\*

\`\`\`yaml  
POST /chat  
Content-Type: application/json

Request:  
{  
  "message": "string (required, max 2000 chars)",  
  "session\_id": "string (optional)"  
}

Response (200 OK):  
{  
  "success": true,  
  "response": "string",  
  "sources": \["string"\],  
  "session\_id": "string"  
}

Response (400 Bad Request):  
{  
  "success": false,  
  "error": {  
    "code": "VALIDATION\_ERROR",  
    "message": "string"  
  }  
}

Response (500 Internal Server Error):  
{
